identifier: 'L'}, {x: 236, y: 34, identifier: 'S'}, {x: 237, y: 34, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 238, y: 34, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 239, y: 34, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 240, y: 34, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 241, y: 34, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 242, y: 34, identifier: 'S'}, {x: 243, y: 34, identifier: 'D'}, {x: 244, y: 34, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 245, y: 34, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 246, y: 34, identifier: 'V'}, {x: 247, y: 34, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 248, y: 34, identifier: 'I'}, {x: 249, y: 34, identifier: 'W'}, {x: 250, y: 34, identifier: 'F'}, {x: 251, y: 34, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 252, y: 34, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 253, y: 34, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 254, y: 34, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 255, y: 34, identifier: 'M'}, {x: 256, y: 34, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 257, y: 34, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 258, y: 34, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 280, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 281, y: 15, identifier: 'V'}, {x: 282, y: 15, identifier: 'P'}, {x: 283, y: 15, identifier: 'Y'}, {x: 284, y: 15, identifier: 'T'}, {x: 285, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 286, y: 15, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 287, y: 15, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 288, y: 15, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 289, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 290, y: 15, identifier: 'E'}, {x: 291, y: 15, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 292, y: 15, identifier: 'E'}, {x: 293, y: 15, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 294, y: 15, identifier: 'E'}, {x: 295, y: 15, identifier: 'Y'}, {x: 296, y: 15, identifier: 'A'}, {x: 297, y: 15, identifier: 'I'}, {x: 298, y: 15, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 299, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 300, y: 15, identifier: 'F'}, {x: 301, y: 15, identifier: 'I'}, {x: 302, y: 15, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 303, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 304, y: 15, identifier: 'D'}, {x: 305, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 306, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 307, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 308, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 309, y: 15, identifier: 'I'}, {x: 310, y: 15, identifier: 'S'}, {x: 311, y: 15, identifier: 'A'}, {x: 312, y: 15, identifier: 'A'}, {x: 313, y: 15, identifier: 'T'}, {x: 314, y: 15, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 315, y: 15, identifier: 'L'}, {x: 316, y: 15, identifier: 'S'}, {x: 317, y: 15, identifier: 'E'}, {x: 318, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 319, y: 15, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 320, y: 15, identifier: 'V'}, {x: 321, y: 15, identifier: 'T'}, {x: 322, y: 15, identifier: 'I'}, {x: 323, y: 15, identifier: 'W'}, {x: 324, y: 15, identifier: 'F'}, {x: 325, y: 15, identifier: 'Q'}, {x: 326, y: 15, identifier: 'N'}, {x: 327, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 328, y: 15, identifier: 'R'}, {x: 329, y: 15, identifier: 'V'}, {x: 330, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}, {x: 331, y: 15, identifier: 'D'}, {x: 332, y: 15, identifier: 'K'}],
      pointRadius : 5,
      backgroundColor: 'rgba(153, 102, 255, 0.5)',
    },
    
  ];

  const [activeAdditionalDatasets, setActiveAdditionalDatasets] = useState(
    new Array(initialAdditionalDatasets.length).fill(false)
  );

  const [additionalDatasets, setAdditionalDatasets] = useState(initialAdditionalDatasets);

  const [colorPickerVisible, setColorPickerVisible] = useState(
    new Array(initialAdditionalDatasets.length).fill(false)
  );

  const toggleAdditionalDataset = (index) => {
    setActiveAdditionalDatasets(prev =>
      prev.map((isActive, idx) => idx === index ? !isActive : isActive)
    );
  };

  const handleColorChange = (index, color) => {
    setAdditionalDatasets(prev => 
      prev.map((dataset, idx) => 
        idx === index ? { ...dataset, backgroundColor: color.hex } : dataset
      )
    );
    setColorPickerVisible(prev => prev.map((visible, idx) => (idx === index ? false : visible)));
  };

  const showColorPicker = (index) => {
    setColorPickerVisible(prev => prev.map((visible, idx) => (idx === index ? true : visible)));
  };

  const hideColorPicker = (index) => {
    setColorPickerVisible(prev => prev.map((visible, idx) => (idx === index ? false : visible)));
  };

  const additionalDatasetsWithState = additionalDatasets.map((dataset, index) => ({
    ...dataset,
    hidden: !activeAdditionalDatasets[index],
  }));

  const data = {
    datasets: [
      ...initialDatasets.map(dataset => ({
        ...dataset,
        hidden: !activeDatasets.includes(dataset.label),
      })),
      ...horizontalLineDatasets, // Include horizontal line datasets
      ...additionalDatasetsWithState, // Include additional datasets
    ]
  };

  const clearAllDatasets = () => {
    setActiveDatasets([]);
    setActiveAdditionalDatasets(new Array(additionalDatasets.length).fill(false));
  };

  const options = {
    scales: {
      x: {
        type: 'linear',
        position: 'bottom',
        title: {
          display: true,
          text: 'Amino Acid Position',
        },
        ticks: {
          padding: 10, // Add padding between ticks and labels
        }
      },
      y: {
        title: {
          display: true,
          text: 'Protein',
        },
        ticks: {
          min: 1,
          max: yLabels.length,
          stepSize: 1,
          autoSkip: false,
          padding: 10, // Add padding between ticks and labels
          callback: function(value) {
            return yLabels[value - 1]; // Adjust to get the correct label
          }
        }
      }
    },
    layout: {
      padding: {
        left: 10,
        right: 10,
        top: 10,
        bottom: 10
      }
    },
    plugins: {
      tooltip: {
        callbacks: {
          label: function(tooltipItem) {
            const dataset = data.datasets[tooltipItem.datasetIndex];
            const dataPoint = dataset.data[tooltipItem.dataIndex];
            return `${dataPoint.identifier}: (x: ${dataPoint.x}, y: ${dataPoint.y})`;
          }
        }
      },
      legend: {
        display: true,
        onClick: () => null, // Disable legend click interactions
        labels: {
          filter: (legendItem) => {
            if (legendItem.text.startsWith('Line')) {
              return false; // Exclude lines from legend
            }
            return (
              activeDatasets.includes(legendItem.text) ||
              activeAdditionalDatasets[additionalDatasets.findIndex(d => d.label === legendItem.text)]
            );
          }
        }
      }
    }
  };

  return (
    <div>
      <LegendDropdown
        datasets={initialDatasets}
        activeDatasets={activeDatasets}
        toggleDataset={toggleDataset}
        clearAll={clearAllDatasets} // Pass the clearAllDatasets function as a prop
      />
      {/* Additional dataset toggles */}
      <div style={{ display: 'flex', justifyContent: 'center', gap: '10px', marginTop: '10px' }}>
        {additionalDatasets.map((dataset, index) => (
          <div
            key={dataset.label}
            style={{ textAlign: 'center', position: 'relative' }}
            onMouseEnter={() => showColorPicker(index)}
            onMouseLeave={() => hideColorPicker(index)}
          >
            <button
              onClick={() => toggleAdditionalDataset(index)}
              style={{
                backgroundColor: activeAdditionalDatasets[index] ? dataset.backgroundColor : 'lightgray',
                color: 'white',
                border: 'none',
                borderRadius: '5px',
                padding: '5px 10px',
                cursor: 'pointer',
                transition: 'background-color 0.5s ease',
              }}
            >
              {dataset.label}
            </button>
            {colorPickerVisible[index] && (
              <div style={{ position: 'absolute', zIndex: 1, top: '40px' }}>
                <ChromePicker
                  color={dataset.backgroundColor}
                  onChangeComplete={(color) => handleColorChange(index, color)}
                  disableAlpha
                />
              </div>
            )}
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* Chart container with padding */}
      <div style={{ margin: '30px' }}>
        <Scatter data={data} options={options} />
      </div>
    </div>
  );
};

export default ScatterPlot_Ranked;
